        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol,iReq,-1.0) ! expect x(jCol) to be positive
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol+1,iReq,-1.0) ! expect x(jCol) to be positive
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol+j,iRqkTn,q4   ) ! link kTn received at iDNod
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol+j,iRqfBt,1.0  ) ! link fBtu received at iDNod
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol+j,iRqWSC,f4) ! link SO2Content*fBtu at iDNod
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol+j,iRqSO2,r4 & !  link SO2/kT received at iDNod
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol+j,iReq,StoDkT(iLink)) ! link kTn shipped via iRout
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol-1,iReq,-1.0) ! kTn shipped via iRout in bounds
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol  ,iReq,-1.0) ! kTn shipped via iRout above UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0) ! iCol has this state's SO2<UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0) ! iCol has this state's SO2>UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol+j,iReq,r4*p4)
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0) ! iCol has group's SO2<UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0) ! iCol has group's SO2>UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol,iReq,1.0) ! jCol has this state's SO2<UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol,iReq,1.0) ! jCol has this state's SO2>UB
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0)
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(iCol,iReq,-1.0)
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call AssignCNWAMtx(jCol,iReq,1.0) ! iSNod kT supplied from basin
     64 returncnwamtx
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call ReturnCNWAMtx(j,i,r4)
     65 returncnwamtx
        cnwmsubs.f90         |call ReturnCNWAMtx(j,i,r4)
